ACTION_NONE 0x61680000 /**< Denotes that no action is assigned or performed. */ 
ACTION_TIMER 0x61680001 /**< Used to indicate only the timer event was received. */ 
ACTION_KEYPRESS 0x61680002 /**< Notifies the driver / application, that a key / button was pressed */ 
ACTION_MOUSERELEASE 0x61680003 /**< Indicates that mouse action (left) button was released. */ 
ACTION_MOUSEDOWN 0x61680004 /**< Indicates that the mouse action (left) button was clicked. */ 
ACTION_MOUSEMOVE 0x61680005 /**< Indicates that the mouse cursor has moved. */ 
ACTION_CLICK 0x61680006 /**< Indicates that the control has been clicked. */ 
ACTION_DRAG 0x61680007 /**< Indicates that the control has been dragged. */ 
ACTION_CHANGE 0x61680008 /**< Indicates that the value of the control has been changed. */ 
ACTION_MOUSEOVER 0x61680009 /**< Indicates that the mouse cursor is over a GUI element. \note Currently not implemented. */ 
ACTION_MOUSEOUT 0x6168000a /**< Indicates that the mouse cursor is out a GUI element area. \note Currently not implemented. */ 
ACTION_EXIT 0x6168000b /**< Used to indicate the application needs to exit the ExecuteDisplayLoop(). */ 
ACTION_FRAME_CHANGED 0x61680300 /**< Indicates that a Frame element has changed. \note For internal use only. */ 
ACTION_BUTTON_CLICKED 0x61680400 /**< Indicates that a BUTTON has been clicked. Can be used along with CALLBACK handler type to notify the user of GUI driver. */ 
ACTION_CHECKBOX_CLICKED 0x61680500 /**< Indicates that a CHECKBOX has been checked/unchecked. Can be used along with CALLBACK handler type to notify the user of GUI driver. */ 
ACTION_DROPBOX_EXPANDED 0x61680600 /**< Indicates that a DROPBOX has been expanded. \note For internal use only. Currently not implemented. */ 
ACTION_DROPBOX_CHANGED 0x61680601 /**<Indicates that Options in a DROPBOX has been changed. Can be used along with CALLBACK handler type to notify the user of GUI driver. DataA parameter in ACTION_INFO will indicate the index of the selected option. */ 
ACTION_INPUT_CHANGED 0x61680800 /**< Indicates that INPUT string has been changed. Can be used along with CALLBACK handler type to notify the user of GUI driver. DataA parameter in ACTION_INFO will hold the pointer to the string. */ 
ACTION_LINK_CLICKED 0x61680b00 /**< Indicates that a LINK has been clicked. Can be used along with CALLBACK handler type to notify the user of GUI driver. */ 
ACTION_RADIOGROUP_CHANGED 0x61680e00 /**< Indicates that Options in a RADIOGROUP has been changed. Can be used along with CALLBACK handler type to notify the user of GUI driver. DataA parameter in ACTION_INFO will indicate the index of the selected option. */ 
ACTION_SCROLLBAR_CHANGE 0x61681100 /**< Indicates that a SCROLLBAR position has changed. Currently used for internal use only. */ 
ACTION_SLIDER_CHANGE 0x61681200 /**< Indicates that Options in a SLIDER bar position has been altered. Can be used along with CALLBACK handler type to notify the user of GUI driver. DataA parameter in ACTION_INFO will indicate the position (0 - MAX <value assigned. by default 100>) of the slider bar. */ 
ACTION_SPIN_CHANGED 0x61681300 /**< Indicates that Spin value has been changed. Can be used along with CALLBACK handler type to notify the user of GUI driver. DataA parameter in ACTION_INFO will hold the new value to the spin. */ 
ACTION_SUBMENU_EXPANDED 0x61681400 /**< Indicates that a SUBMENU has been expanded. For internal use only. \note Currently not implemented. */ 
ACTION_SUBMENU_ITEM_SELECTED 0x61681401 /**< Indicates SUBMENU item has been selected. Can be used along with CALLBACK handler type to notify the user of GUI driver. DataA parameter in ACTION_INFO will indicate the index of the selected option. */ 
ACTION_TOGGLE_SWITCHED 0x61681700 /**< Indicates that a TOGGLE position has been switched. Can be used along with CALLBACK handler type to notify the user of GUI driver. DataA parameter in ACTION_INFO will indicate the selected option. */ 
ACTION_TREE_EXPANDED 0x61681800 /**< Indicates that a TREE has been expanded. For internal use only. \note Currently not implemented. */
